 This is the first study in the world of its kind
 pregnancy main doodh pine se badhegi bacchon kii lambaai
 
 
 Gestational diabetes mellitus is considered a serious complication of pregnancy
 isamen garbhavastha main blad sugar par niyantran nahin rah paata
 Complications of this type of diabetes include weight gain, premature birth of a baby, loss of blood sugar, etc
 aise main janm lene vaale bachche main bhi bade hokar tip 2 diabetes se grast hone kaa khatra bad jaataa he
 "our study is the first of its kind in which there is strong evidence of the relationship between gestational diabetes and 'what season in which pregnancy took place'," said Petra Varberg, associated with the University of Adelaide's Robinson Research Institute
 'ye study 2007 se 2011 ke bich kii gai
 It showed that in 2007 the number of pregnant women affected by gestational diabetes was 4
 9 fisadi thi jo 2011 main bad kar 7
 2%
 pregnancy main thyroid hona ban saktaa he samasya
 
 
 The study also revealed that women who conceive during winter are at higher risk of gestational diabetes during pregnancy
 is tarah kii kul garbhvatee mahilaon main 6
 Gestational diabetes was found in 6 percent of women

 Almost 700 years before the birth of Jesus, almost all people worshiped the deity Jupiter in the continent of Europe and especially in the countries of the Mediterranean coast
 jupiter-poojak apane devtaa ko sarvashaktimaan maanate the
 The people of Europe believed that the creatures of the world get happiness and peace only through the grace of the Jupiter, and the anger of the wicked is destroyed by his anger
 isi kaaran ye log jupiter kii murti ko kahin safed sangemarmar kii shant or gambhir mudra main tathaa haathon main jwaala liye rakshak ke rup main or kahin kaale pathar kii raudra rup main banavaate the
 In Greece and Rome, Jupiter was worshiped from house to house
 kintu faras ke akramanakariyon ne yunaan desh kii rajdhani athens nagar ke lagbhag sabhi dev-mandiron ko tod daalaa athwa aag laga kar raakh kar diya tha

 aaj bhi in nasht-bhrasht pavitra dev mandiron ke khandhiron ke neeche kii bhoomi raakhadaar milti he

 in mandiron ko banane main athens ke shaasha periclij, karigar ikatines tathaa sangatraash fedias kaa haath tha

 aaj bhi athens ke dev-mandir sansar ke sarvshereshth bhawan maane jate hai, kintu ye bhawan 1000 varsh tak dev-mandir rahe

 sansar ke kone-kone se aakar kushal karigar or santagarash in dev-murtiyon dwaara fedias kii kaary-kushalta kaa adhyayan karte hai
 The name of Phidias began to become famous about 464 years before the birth of Jesus
 athens kaa shaasha periclij uskaa ghanishtha mitra tha or usne fedias ko athens ke sabhi dev-mandiron, murtiyon tathaa smarakon ke banane kaa kaam saunp diya tha
 Phidias was not an ordinary man
 vah prachinkaal kaa suvikhyath sangatraash tha
 This remarkable man not only had full ability to use his tools, he also had full knowledge of subjects which were related to his business, such as history, poetry, fables, line-mathematics, light-science etc
 sabase pehle fedias ne hi unani logon ko prakruti kaa purnataya anukaran karne kii shiksha di thi
 The Greeks had great respect for the work and mentorship of this unique artist
 usne minerva devi kii badi hi utkrisht murti kaa nirmaan kiya tha
 Made of ivory and gold, this statue is 39 feet high
 is murti main fedias ne devi kii dhaal par apana tathaa apane mitra periclij kaa chitra bhi khoda he or isi ke kaaran athens nivasee use irshyaa karne lage the
 He therefore accused Fidias of abducting the goods of the goddess
 fedias athens-nivaasiyon ke is bure vyavhaar se dukhi hokar olympia chalaa gaya
 Going there he built that statue of Jupiter deity of Olympia
 vah kala kii ek vilakshan kriti thi or uski gananaa sansar ke saat aashcharyo main hui
 This statue was made 30 feet high with ivory and gold and the proportion of each part of it was perfectly fine
 iskaa vaibhav bhi mandir ke vaibhav jaisaa hi tha
 Its beauty made the religion of Greece far more aesthetic
 vah murti fedias kii sarvotkrisht kriti thi or is murti ke kaaran hi sansar ke itihaas main fedias tathaa yunaan desh kaa naam sadaa ke liye amar ho gaya
 Such a great Tyagi and scholar artist was accused by his countrymen for the second time that Phidias had committed a wrongdoing by digging a portrait of himself and his friend Pariklij on the shield of the idol of the goddess
